<p>
Here you can find more about a project that I launched with a friend on
October 2025
</p>
<p>
Gifted is a way to offer an original gift made with photographs that fit
your budget.
</p>
<p>
You can upload on our website photographs of a loved one. Then, you fix
your price.
</p>
<p>
A week after, you receive a wooden box with things that are dear to your
loved one, including photographs.
</p>
<p>
An exclusive experience generated by AI which creates a story around the
person.
</p>
